Coffee Talk

Posted on 2024-02-09

Coffee Talk

I want to find a text game to practice my spoken English, and I have already played this one for a long time on my SteamDeck. So, I tried extracting the text from the game’s source file and found out that it uses a CSV file to save all localized texts. Therefore, I wrote a simple script to extract English and Chinese into a Markdown file.

Script

The inGameLocalization.csv file is under steamapps/common/Coffee\ Talk/CoffeeTalk_Data/StreamingAssets, and you can simply check all properties with pandas.

Here is the code output markdown file:

It is possible to show English with subtitles in-game, based on what this man did. However, The file he provided isn’t available and I have already tried my changed file on Steamdeck and it didn’t work. I will try again if I have time.

Considering they use braces to change the font, I use \{[^{}]*\} to delete all the patterns of {*}).

Text

Welco— Oh, it’s you.
欢迎光－－哦，是你啊。
Hey cherium, how’s the night so far?
嗨，cherium。今晚还好吗？

和平时一样，还挺平静。

不过我们遇到了一个小问题。

Yes.

这样就能用多出来的一周时间来修改和润色。
Sounds like a plan.
听起来不错。
If you can pull it off.
前提是你能够做到。

知道啦，知道啦。你没必要那么冷嘲热讽嘛。

来杯热巧克力怎么样？

和今晚的天气很搭哦。

Thank you.
谢谢。
So warm.

Hmm…

You know, in my native language…
你知不知道，在我们种族的母语里……
… we call the color brown, “chocolate.”
……我们把棕色称为“巧克力色”。
Because the color looks like… well, chocolate.
因为这种颜色看起来……和巧克力一样。
And this drink doesn’t look brown at all.
而这杯看起来一点也不棕色。
Oh my, I’m sorry.
哎呀，很抱歉。

一定是我弄错了。

You went from empty to three customers in one night.

I thought this place would be more crowded.
我还以为这家店会更热闹呢。
Considering it’s the only coffee shop that’s still open after midnight around here.
毕竟这一带午夜后仍然开张的咖啡馆就只有这里了。
Because it’s the only coffee shop that still opens past midnight, it’s mostly empty.
正因为这是唯一一家只在午夜之后开张的咖啡馆，所以才没什么人啦。
Now that you mention it…
说到这一点……
Is it good for business, having the coffee shop only open at night?
这样只在大半夜开店，生意真的好做吗？
Definitely not.
当然是有百害而无一利。
Yup, what she said.
嗯，和她说的一样。
Then why?
那为什么要这么做呢？
I just love doing it.
因为我喜欢这样吧。
And there’s always someone longing for a warm drink at this hour.
而且这种时候总会有人需要一杯热饮的。
That’s fascinating.
真有意思。

这个问题可能有些失礼……

但你在这种情况下经营这家咖啡馆，要靠什么维持生计？
That’s a secret.

cherium here is damn rich, that’s the secret.
秘密就是，这位cherium特别有钱。
Oh, really…?
哦，真的吗？
She’s exaggerating.
她说得太夸张了。
Don’t worry about it, cherium can manage.

I’m sure this place isn’t going bankrupt anytime soon.

So you’ll still have a weird, quiet place to meet up at night.
所以你在每个夜晚都能找到这么一个古怪而安静的聚会场所。
That’s good to hear.
那还挺不错的。
By the way, are you a regular here?

I’m a writer who works best at night and in a coffee shop.

Not so many options for that.
这种组合可没多少选择哦。

She’s a pretty good writer, you know.

You can find some of her stories in The Evening Whispers.

What kind of things do you cover?

嘿，我平时玩游戏的时候你不都挺爱看的吗。
I enjoyed watching you, not the game.
我爱看的是你，不是游戏啊。
Too bad I didn’t introduce you to Myrtle just now, Baileys.
哇，可惜我刚刚没有把你介绍给默特尔哎，贝里斯。
She worked on the game.
她有参与那个系列的开发哦。
Really?
真的吗？
Oh well, I’ll be visiting this place more often.
哈，好吧，反正之后我会更常来店里的。
I’ll probably meet her again, one of these days.
总有一天还会遇到她的吧。
You probably will.
嗯，应该会的。
Now go, you lovebirds!
所以你们这对小情侣可以出发啦。
You don’t want to miss the movie.
可别错过电影咯。
All right. Catch up with you later, Freya!
好，那以后再聊，芙蕾雅。
Bye, cherium.
再见，cherium。
Enjoy the movie.
祝两位观影愉快。
There they go.
看看他们两个。
I’m so happy for them.
真是为他们感到高兴啊。
They’ve still got a long way to go…
他们未来要走的路还很长……
And probably a lot of obstacles in their path…
恐怕还会有很多障碍吧。
But they’re moving forward.
但他们正在一步一步向前走了。
Yes.
是这样没错。
How will you write their story?
你会怎么写他们的故事呢？
As it is.
就写现实的样子啊。
It’s beautiful enough.
已经足够美好了不是吗？
And it has enough drama.
戏剧效果也够足。
Hah!
哈。
That’s one way to put it.
这么说也没错。
I hope not.
我希望不是。
What do you mean?
哎，什么意思啊？
I’m waiting for Lua.
我在等露亚。
Oh?
哎？
How are things between you two lately?
你们两个最近怎么样啊？
…
……
I haven’t spoke to her since the last time we met.
我们上次碰面后，我都还没和她说上过话。
Did you try to make contact?
你有试着联系她吗？
She blocked my number…
她屏蔽了我的号码……
And blocked me on all her social media.
还在所有的社交网络上拉黑了我。
So… how do you know she’ll be here?
那你怎么知道她会不会来呢？
I don’t.
我不知道。
…
……
I left her a letter at her office and her apartment.
我给她的公司和她的住处都寄去了一封信。
I told her I’ll be waiting at Coffee Talk until midnight.
告诉她我会在这里等到午夜。
I’ve been here since the place opened…
今天这里一开门我就来等了……
And I’m planning to wait until… I don’t know.
我会一直等到……我也不知道什么时候。
What are you planning to do if she comes?
如果她真的来了，你有什么打算呢？
Set things straight.
把话好好说清。
I was a fool.
之前是我太傻。
I need to make her believe in me…
我需要让她相信我……
I need to make her believe in… us.
我需要让她相信……我们。
And if she doesn’t come?
她要是不来呢？
…
……
I’m moving to Austin.
我就搬去奥斯汀。
What?!
哎？！
Why?
为什么啊？
It’s cheaper to live there.
那里生活更便宜。
I’m just a freelancer, remember?
你没忘了我是个自由职业者吧？
But it’s really far!
可是那离这里好远啊。
That’s the point.
就是要远一点。
If she doesn’t come tonight…
如果今晚她不来……
It’s a clear sign that I should move on.
那就再清楚不过了，我必须得放下这段感情才行。
And it’d be too hard to do that…
而只要我人还住在西雅图……
As long as I still live in Seattle.
我就不太可能做到这一点。
…
……
Hey, don’t look at me like that.
嘿，别拿那样的表情看着我嘛。
I’ll fit in well in Texas.
德州会很适合我的。
That’s where my favorite band are from, after all.
那里毕竟是我最喜欢的乐队的发源地。
If you look at it that way, it does suit you.
如果你这么想的话，那确实挺适合啦。
You’re still going to do freelance design?
那你还是做自由设计吗？
Yeah.
是啊。
And you never know… I might try doing my own stuff.
而且说不定……也会尝试做点自己想做的东西。
Like what?
比如说呢？
Fashion, maybe…
服装设计……
Or comics…
或者漫画……
We’ll see.
到时再看吧。
I can only wish you luck, then.
那我也只能祝你好运了。
Well… I’d prefer it if Lua came tonight.
不过我还是希望露亚会过来。
…
……
Let’s talk about something else while we’re waiting for her.
在我们等她的时候，还是聊点别的吧！
Sure.
好啊。
No… you didn’t!
不是吧，你真那么做了啊！
Yep! That’s what I did!
对，就是那样。
Then I just told them, if they don’t pay me…
然后我就告诉他们，如果他们到了合同里写的时限……
… by the deadline mentioned in the contract…
……还不把钱打到我的账户里的话……
… I’m going to take this matter to court.
……我就去法院告他们。
Oh, wow!
哇噻。
Wouldn’t that have just cost you more, though?
但是诉讼费用会不会让你花更多的钱呢？
I was a pretty impulsive guy, remember?
你忘了吗？我就是那么冲动的性格啊。
Yeah…
看起来……
She’s not coming.
她是不会来了。
I guess that’s it for me, then.
我想我也该认命了。
…
……
When are you leaving for Austin?
你什么时候搬去奥斯汀呢？
Next week.
下个星期。
That soon?!
这么快啊？！
I’ve been living at my friend’s house for almost a month.
我已经在朋友家里借住了快一个月了。
I don’t have much by way of belongings, anyway.
而且我也没有多少随身物品。
So, I guess… I’ll leave now.
那我想……我该回去了。
Gotta pack my one backpack.
还要好好打包一下我那一个背包。
And probably have some farewell drinks with Farron and the others.
或许还要跟法隆和其他几个人喝个散伙酒。
Your housemate?
那是你室友吧？
More like my host.
不如说是我的房东啊。
Hehehe!
嘿嘿嘿。
Thank you for the company and the drinks, cherium.
谢谢你的陪伴和饮料，cherium。
The pleasure was mine.
是我该谢谢您的惠顾。
Please do visit this place if you’re in town.
将来再来这座城市的时候，还请再到店里来转转。
I sure hope that won’t happen anytime soon.
我想短时间内都不会再来了吧。
Ciao, folks!
拜拜了，伙计们！
Bye.
拜拜。
Good bye.
再见。
I feel sad for them.
他们两个的事我觉得好伤心啊。
Sometimes… things don’t go the way we want them to.
世事……并不总能如愿的，更何况是我们这些旁人的愿望呢。
How will you write their story in the book?
你在书里会怎么写他们的故事？
As it is, probably.
应该就和现实一样吧。
It doesn’t have a good ending.
没有美满的结局。
But it’s bittersweet.
是个苦乐参半的故事啊。
And it’s the truth.
这何尝不是人生呢。
I’m sure a lot of people can relate…
他们所经历的这些事情……
To what they’ve been through.
会有很多人感同身受吧。
That’s one way to put it.
这么说也没错。
By the way…
对了……
I haven’t seen your final draft.
我还没有看过你最后的稿子呢。
May I read it?
可以让我拜读一下吗？
Sure.
当然啦。
I brought an extra copy.
我特地多带了一份副本哦。
Let’s see…
那我就开始了……
Hmm…
哼嗯……
The main character is a time traveler?
所以主角是个时间旅行者？
Subtly.
只是这么暗示。
I mention it just enough to raise suspicion.
我明写的部分只有一点点，但肯定能引发讨论。
Where did you get the inspiration for the character?
这个角色的创意是从哪里来的呢？
You know the answer.
答案你很清楚哦。
Why would I?
我怎么会清楚？
Either you’re smart enough to get what I mean…
我觉得吧，有两种可能。要么你够聪明，知道我是什么意思……
Or you already know what my answer is…
要么你已经知道我的答案是什么……
(gulp)
（咽口水）
Don’t think about it too much, it’s only a story.
哎呀，别想那么多嘛。只是小说而已啦。
Anyway…
总而言之呢……
…
……
What’s that look for?
你那是什么表情啊？
You haven’t told me about any of our other friends here.
你还没有告诉我咖啡馆里其他朋友的情况呢。
How are they doing?
他们过得怎么样呀？
You only skipped coming for ten days.
你只不过十天没来而已啊。
What do you expect?
你觉得会有什么大事吗？
Come on, they played an important part in my writing process, remember?
哎呀拜托啦，别忘了他们在我的写作过程中扮演了重要的角色哦。
Well…
好吧……
There are some updates about the regulars.
我可以跟你说说几位常客的近况。
Tell me, tell me!
快说快说啦！
Where should we start?
嗯，该从哪里开始说起呢？
So, she found out, huh?
所以，她发现了么？
Clever as usual.
果然和往常一样敏锐。
In some timelines… yeah.
对……至少在某些时间线里。
But I have to ask you this…
但我想问你的问题是……
Why?
为什么？
Why what?
什么为什么？
Why do all this?
为什么要做这一切？
Opening the café…
开咖啡馆……
Connecting people…
连起人与人之间的关系……
I just… like to make sure things go all right.
我只是想要确保一切都顺顺利利。
Besides…
而且……
Yes?
什么？
I also have to make sure…
我也要保证……
That I’ll exist on Earth.
自己会存在在地球上才行啊。
Hah!
哈哈！
That’s one hell of an important task indeed.
那可确实是个重要任务了。
It is.
当然。
Welcome.
欢迎光临。
Hello, cherium.
你好，cherium。
Good evening, sir.
晚上好，先生。
Umm… Have we met before?
那个……我们见过吗？
I’m sure this is your first time here.
我很确定您应该是第一次来。
Of course I’ve been here.
我当然不是第一次来了。
In fact, I’ve worked here before.
过去我还在这里打过工呢。
What?
哎？
Wait…
等一下……
No way.
不可能吧。
Is that really you?
真的是你们……是你吗？
It’s been awhile…
很久不见咯……
You’ve changed … a bit too much.
你的变化……有点太大了。
I’ve learned a lot about how to live with your people since then.
从那以后，我可是学习了很多如何与你们相处的方法。
I assume it was a success, then?
那么那件事成功了么？
Multiple successes.
不止一次。
What’s with the new look, then?
那新造型是怎么回事？
Just trying to blend in.
只是试着融入这里啊。
It seems like an Earthling immigration agency is after me.
因为地球移民署似乎在追查我。
Now that you mention it…
你这么一提……
Somebody did visit this place looking for you.
确实有人来这里找过你。
When was it?
什么时候的事？
Not so long after your second visit here.
大约你第二次来之后没多久。
Was he a bald guy in a suit?
是个西装革履的光头男子吗？
Yes.
对。
That F.I.R.E. agent…
哦，那位F.I.R.E.特工。
You’ve seen him?
你见过他？
Yes… Thankfully, I’ve changed my appearance since then.
是的，幸亏之后我就改了样貌。
By the way…
对了……
You can drop the act in front of me.
在我面前你就不用假装啦。
…
……
So, you finally noticed.
你终于注意到了吗。
To think that such power can be born from our kind.
真没想到，我们种族的后代竟能拥有这样的能力。
You’re good with your act, though.
不过你的演技还真不错。
It took a few tries…
我也是熟能生巧啊。
But there are some timelines where I…
不过还是有那么几次……
…
……
Where I forget to pretend that I don’t have…
我忘了假装自己……
Some knowledge of certain stuff.
其实应该还不知道一些事情。
Heh, interesting.
呵呵，那还挺有意思。
Now I’m curious to know about those mistakes…
你这么说，我可就好奇那些失误出现在哪里了……
Well, it happened a few times…
嗯，有过几次吧……
First, when Freya told me about her meeting in the elevator…
首先是芙蕾雅告诉我她在电梯里见面的事……
Then, it was the first time Rachel visited this place.
然后是瑞秋第一次来的时候。
And the last one involved you on your second visit.
还有一次是你第二次来的时候。
Huh?
哎？
Oh, and there was another one right after Freya got her draft approved.
啊对了，还有芙蕾雅的初稿通过了之后有一次。
Can you show it to me?
嗯，能详细和我说说吗？
Assuming you know how I communicate with my kind.
如果你知道我和同类是怎样交流的话。
Never tried it, but let’s see…
我还从来没有试过，不过这就来试试看吧……
